# Key | Anytype Docs

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-7cc068865effff17f378946e2f17c5263590067e%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ad0253ff&sv=2)

When you create your vault, you will receive your very own 12 word mnemonic phrase. This phrase is generated on-device and is the only way to access your vault and decrypt your data.

Your Key functions as your login and passphrase at the same time. This mnemonic represents your master key generated upon signup, similar to a Bitcoin wallet.

Changing it is impossible, and it's extremely important you keep it safe. You can access it at any time by navigating to the Key section in your [Vault Settings](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/settings/account-and-data)
.

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/vault-and-key/key#dont-forget-to-save-it)

Don't forget to save it!

We do not save a copy of your key, which means that if it's lost, we are not able to assist with recovering your vault. For this reason, we recommend making a digital backup or writing it down and keeping it somewhere safe.

You will need this key each time you login on a new device.

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/vault-and-key/key#if-youve-lost-your-key)

If you've lost your Key

Encrypted apps work in a way that puts the responsibility for your personal data entirely in your hands. Since these apps are completely anonymous, we can't identify or delete individual Vaults. Even if we could, we wouldn't be able to verify with certainty if we're talking to the actual Vault owner or someone else.

If you've been logged out of Anytype, and haven't stored your Key somewhere else, you only have two options to recover your Key:

1.  If you're still logged in on another device, you might still be able to restore your Vault. Just open the app there and copy the Key from your settings.
    
2.  You can also try recovering your Key from your [OS Key storage manager](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/faqs#how-to-recover-my-key-from-my-os-key-storage-manager)
    .
    

[PreviousVaultchevron-left](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/vault-and-key)
[NextChannelschevron-right](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/vault-and-key/space)

Last updated 3 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Don't forget to save it!](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/vault-and-key/key#dont-forget-to-save-it)
    
*   [If you've lost your Key](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/vault-and-key/key#if-youve-lost-your-key)
    

Was this helpful?

# Mission | Anytype Docs

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-8a08080b5e0c258a009d5dad6573b2375491a88b%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2feeb7a7&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/readme/mission#why-are-we-building-anytype)

Why are we building Anytype

We imagine a world where our fundamental digital freedoms are sacred: the privacy of thought; the freedom to connect with those we trust; and, the freedom to participate in the governance of our digital creations.

We believe that these freedoms are as important to the world of bits, as fundamental human rights are to the world of atoms.

circle-info

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/readme/mission#were-building-an-alternative-for-those-who-value-freedom-and-trust-for-ourselves)

We’re building an alternative for those who value freedom and trust — for ourselves.

The current web and much of the software we use do not respect these digital freedoms. In the architecture of the current web, application developers are the keepers of our keys; they control the keys to users’ accounts.

As the gatekeepers of our accounts, they determine who has access, who does not, and how information is distributed.

With so much of our lives lived online, we are driven to construct an alternative.

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/readme/mission#cooperation-as-a-magic-wand)

Cooperation as a magic wand

Cooperation is our superpower - our remarkable ability to advance our knowledge and well-being by working together. It has enabled us, an unassuming species from sub-Saharan Africa, to inhabit locations all across the planet, build the pyramids, discover atoms and DNA, and even venture into space.

We believe that tools for thought, freedom, and trust are what have enabled us to create all the art, science, technologies, devices, and structures we see around us. They allowed us to build cities and reach for the stars.

circle-info

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/readme/mission#our-mission-is-to-empower-sustainable-cooperation-by-building-tools-for-thought-freedom-and-trust)

Our mission is to empower sustainable cooperation by building tools for thought, freedom and trust.

To achieve this level of cooperation, we mastered language. Language was a tool for thought that allowed us to create stories, some of which are social innovations - powerful inter-subjective realities that exist only when enough people believe in them. Humans found a way to use these stories to build trust and freedom at the same time. To achieve greater cooperation, we need both. If we have trust but lack freedom, it results in a dictatorship; if we have a lot of freedom but lack trust, it leads to anarchy.

We see the web as the main tool for thought, freedom and trust today and our aim is to upgrade it:

*   as a tool for thought by bringing graph as a universal language of data
    
*   as a tool for freedom by embedding universal digital freedoms
    
*   as a tool for trust by building a decentralized layer of trust that supports governance of the positive sum game that the web creates
    

We are of the view that with better tools for thought, freedom, and trust, we could accomplish even more. We could chart a course towards true sustainability, with cooperation at its core.

[PreviousWelcomechevron-left](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs)
[NextInstallchevron-right](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/install-and-setup)

Last updated 3 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Why are we building Anytype](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/readme/mission#why-are-we-building-anytype)
    
*   [Cooperation as a magic wand](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/readme/mission#cooperation-as-a-magic-wand)

# Collaboration | Anytype Docs

You can now find the Members submenu in the Channel Settings menu of each channel you’ve created. Clicking here allows you to generate an invite link for the channel that can be sent to anyone.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-ead46ab913dd703454c4758051a144cb74e3d7ed%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fe98c565&sv=2)

There are three types of invitation link: Editor, Viewer, and Request Access. The first two allow users to join the channel directly with specific access, eliminating the need for confirmation by the owner. The third type enables the owner to select the desired level of access after the user has requested it.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-13d1199db87b954ef2e3e4e70ff4d4d64ebe91f0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ab797ec0&sv=2)

When you create a shared channel you are the Channel Owner. The Channel Owner can change any object in the channel, the channel name and settings, and is the only one with rights to add and remove members.

All other members of the Channel have either Viewer or Editor rights. Viewers have read-only access to the Channel, while Editors can edit any object in the Channel or the Channel Name.

From the same menu, you can manage the roles of guests you have invited to your Channel or remove them altogether. Guests who have been removed from a Channel will receive a notification informing them of this.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-e3874a16c8c0b49bddfcc3707cf22a3a710ef0c1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6b20f10b&sv=2)

[PreviousSidebarchevron-left](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/customize-and-edit-the-sidebar)
[NextPublishchevron-right](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/web-publishing)

# Blocks | Anytype Docs

Your object is made up of different types of blocks to organize your information, and the place where all of these Blocks live together is called the Canvas. Anytype's block-based editor works very similarly to that of blogging sites or website builders.

All block styles originate from the command menu, which you can access by either clicking on the orange `+` symbol on the left-hand side of your editor, or typing `/`.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-4a141ebb31724b1a256b37451c8eb50806ce6d96%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a402a94f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor/blocks#style-your-blocks)

Style your Blocks

You can select one block or several at once, and batch edit to create different headings and text styles such as checkboxes, bullets, or numbers.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-127166e916087ff40d25e63ffbd6d9a7a3055581%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=88105e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor/blocks#inline-styling)

Inline Styling

We also support styling individual characters / words inside text blocks.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-7d49a3c8cd582f571c6e30ef933b5132121e620d%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fcfa8640&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor/blocks#columns)

Columns

You can use the grey 'handle' to the left of each block to create parent/child blocks or new columns in your editor by dragging and dropping them.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-6c5e9a7c1c8dae2c18f9e71c2795a4e06c399f2c%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fcb825f9&sv=2)

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-2a9512f571f7bdf84e03bb426a453fdfc24b8b13%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2b58fe9d&sv=2)

[PreviousObjectschevron-left](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor)
[NextLinkschevron-right](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor/linking-objects)

# Collections | Anytype Docs

Collections can be used to organize a variety of different objects and store them in one place.

You are not restricted to viewing only one Object Type at a time, this means you can have multiple different types within one collection.

If you are organizing your meal prep for the week, you might have a list of recipes, as well as ingredients and a shopping list.

The main types you may have could be Recipes and Ingredients.

In a Collection, you can organize all of this Types together seamlessly.

circle-exclamation

The main difference between Queries and Collections is that Queries draw Objects from your entire Graph, whereas Collections work more like a traditional database, where they start empty and you have to add Objects to them manually.

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/sets/collections#adding-objects)

Adding Objects

To add new Objects to a Collection, simply click on the New buttons either in the top right corner or at the bottom of a collection.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-453438e7fcd55ad62c86cf687f303c55567a6e56%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1ebe2aa9&sv=2)

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-67aa1ad1136628a6c94f5f2875d08f4e07ce37d3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=81bdd72e&sv=2)

To add an existing Object to a Collection while in the collection view, you can hover over the Existing object menu option under the arrow menu.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-71b3d70927ec730801863089da1f165bdcd8412c%252Fexisting-objects-to-collection_shadow.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=25856f10&sv=2)

To add an existing Object to a Collection outside of the collection view, you can use the Add to Collection menu option from the object menu.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-f08963acc6f612ae3441b0db254112c0934bd499%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=39dcc0df&sv=2)

[PreviousQuerieschevron-left](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/sets)
[NextSidebarchevron-right](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/customize-and-edit-the-sidebar)

# Open Any Initiative | Magyar | Anytype Docs

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/magyar/kozosseg/join-the-open-source-project#hozzajarulas)

**Hozzájárulás**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Ha fejlesztő vagy és hozzájárulásoddal szeretnéd segíteni az Anytype-ökoszisztéma fejlődését, kérjük tanulmányozd az [erről szólóarrow-up-right](https://github.com/anyproto/.github/blob/main/docs/CONTRIBUTING.md)
 dokumentumot.

Kövess minket a [Github-onarrow-up-right](https://github.com/anyproto)
, csatlakozz [fejlesztői közösségünkhözarrow-up-right](https://github.com/orgs/anyproto/discussions)
 és építsük együtt az Anytype világát!

Ha érdekel, hogy a voksunkat miért az alkalmazás nyílt forráskódú fejlesztése mellett tettük le, az [alábbi oldalonarrow-up-right](https://blog.anytype.io/our-open-philosophy/)
 többet is megtudhatsz.

A fejlesztési licenszekkel kapcsolatos kérdésekkel kapcsolatban [ittarrow-up-right](https://legal.any.coop/)
, technikai kérdésekkel kapcsolatban [ittarrow-up-right](https://tech.anytype.io/)
 találsz bővebb információt.

[PreviousVisszajelzés küldésechevron-left](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/magyar/kozosseg/community-forum/visszajelzes-kuldese)
[NextAz Any fejlesztési idővonalachevron-right](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/magyar/kozosseg/az-any-fejlesztesi-idovonala)

# Publish | Anytype Docs

You can now publish Objects as static web pages (HTTPS links) on your personal subdomain if you have an ANY ID. These pages are uploaded to our servers as unencrypted HTML files.

This is an early version— linked Objects, and blocks like Queries and Collections aren’t supported yet. Multi-page publishing and other enhancements are on the way, and we’d love your feedback to guide these improvements.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-9aa46bd5b80555cd6e7818052d22bd778d3d1d84%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=19f2860b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/web-publishing#encryption)

Encryption

When users use web publishing, we upload objects unencrypted for a number of reasons:

*   Users explicitly choose an object to publish. So we limit the chance of accidental leakage.
    
*   If users want their website to be indexed by search engines, it should be plaintext.
    
*   The solution of decrypting in the browser and including the encryption key in the URL is a bit tricky in the case of multi-object exports.
    
*   We do rendering and caching server-side to limit resource consumption.
    

The object is decrypted locally on the device and then uploaded to the web publishing server in Anyblock format.

If you have files in your object, we include the encryption keys for those files. But because each file has a unique locally-generated encryption key, it doesn't compromise your account in any way.

[PreviousCollaborationchevron-left](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/collaboration)
[NextChatschevron-right](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/chats)

Last updated 3 months ago

Was this helpful?

Was this helpful?

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Közösségi fórum | Magyar | Anytype Docs

[![Logo](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcommunity-static.anytype.io%2Foptimized%2F2X%2F5%2F53bf41b81c8d7f2d475a9e551a4467f3f3d8b8bb_2_32x32.png&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dd222293&sv=2)Anytype CommunityAnytype Communitychevron-right](https://community.anytype.io/)

Közösségünkben számtalan **kategóriát** és **címkét** használunk, melyek segítségével a többi felhasználó - akár hozzád hasonló - észrevételeit, kérdéseit is könnyedén megtalálhatod. A legfőbb kategóriák a következők: Any News (Hírek és közlemények), Any Talk (Benyomások, visszajelzések, javaslatok), Any Help (Segítségnyújtás), Any Requests? (Funkciók kérése), Bug Report (Hibajelentés) és Any Lounge (Kibeszélő)

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/magyar/kozosseg/community-forum#csatlakozas-a-kozosseghez)

Csatlakozás a közösséghez

Ha szeretnél bejegyzéseket közzétenni a fórumban, létre kell hoznod egy felhasználói fiókot.

Ehhez az asztali alkalmazásban kattints a **?** (Súgó) gombra a jobb alsó sarokban, majd válaszd a "[Csatlakozás a közösséghezarrow-up-right](https://community.anytype.io/invites/sig5xTU4ZZ)
" lehetőséget.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fanyproto%2Fdocs%2Fblob%2Fmain%2Fhu_HU%2F.gitbook%2Fassets%2FScreenshot%25202023-08-23%2520at%252017.42.16.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a9a96904&sv=2)

A közösségi fórumot az alkalmazás tetején található menüsorból is elérheted a `Súgó > Hibajelentés` gombra kattintva.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fanyproto%2Fdocs%2Fblob%2Fmain%2Fhu_HU%2F.gitbook%2Fassets%2Fimage%2520%2845%29.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ff6adda5&sv=2)

[PreviousMultiplayer és csomagok: GYIKchevron-left](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/magyar/elofizetes/csomagok-es-arak/multiplayer-es-csomagok-gyik)
[NextHibajelentéschevron-right](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/magyar/kozosseg/community-forum/hibajelentes)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Types | Anytype Docs

Just as in the physical world, Types are useful for defining Objects which are categorically different from one another.

A banana is something inherently different from a sofa. Its functions, properties, and relationships to other objects is more similar to those of apples and oranges, rather than sofas. For this reason, we might categorize apples, oranges, and bananas as _fruit_, whereas sofas would fall into a different category: that of _furniture._

By the same principle, in Anytype there are two important concepts to keep in mind:

1) Every object has a Type, which is defined at the time of Object creation (and can be changed later)

2) Different Types are used to define Objects which are categorically different from each other

Colleagues, friends, and neighbors might all be considered type: _Human_ in your Anytype graph. Here are other examples of Types you might have in your graph:

*   Task
    
*   Note
    
*   Book
    
*   Movie
    
*   Idea
    

It's up to you how narrow or broad you'd like your Types to be, but generally we recommend using general Types for categorizing your Objects, and further refining the use of your Types through [Templates](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/types/templates)
.

You can always view and manage your Types in your channel settings under the Content model section [Channel Settings](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/settings/space-settings#object-types)

Additionally, each Type has an in-built Query which can be accessed by opening the Type from anywhere in the app.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-fed8f1078c9a60e54673ff88612ab5315f26e92c%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a398fdc6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/types#create-a-new-type)

Create a New Type

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/types#creating-types-from-the-sidebar)

Creating Types from the Sidebar

In case you think of a new object type just as you're creating an object, you can create a new type on-the-fly. In this case, use the type selection menu in the same way as the search bar in the Types library. The type will be automatically added to your Types library, while you can proceed with editing the object of your new type.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-877e648d4dde7ce68ca2876e9b8de9b3bc964a2e%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=97a27ae0&sv=2)

You're also able to create new Types directly from the Objects section:

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-f9bba88b9eb489c4497445ef7c331f23eeb7b8f0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ba269468&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/types#creating-types-from-channel-settings)

Creating Types from Channel Settings

Open your [Channels](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/vault-and-key/space)
 settings, and navigate to `Content Model > Object Types`. Afterwards, simply click on `New` button to create a new Type.

From here, you can choose a name, layout, and add templates and properties to the newly created Type.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-324074cd407b1653e41c8af5868d965cc958006c%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d04b16f0&sv=2)

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-9703c2cb89f49ecd76ef409b4d90d3d6f7829c2d%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4dea7afe&sv=2)

If you've decided that this Type is no longer relevant, you can use the context menu (mouse right-click) to delete the Type from your channel. Please proceed with caution; any objects of this type will show an alert if the Type has been removed from your library.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-e3dffc74889c11eb9b23ee8e3dbf73e3c1b2902b%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3177bff5&sv=2)

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-133755e7fcc9b79a77c3ab60c6c35f5cc0dd9b9c%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d9671f2c&sv=2)

[PreviousLinkschevron-left](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor/linking-objects)
[NextPropertieschevron-right](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/types/relations)

# Refund policy | Anytype Docs

1.  You may cancel your subscription at any time and continue using the service until the end of billing cycle.
    
2.  You may request a full refund within 30 days of the initial purchase.
    
3.  The service is non-refundable after 30-days period, and any refund given will be at the sole discretion of the Company.
    
4.  Payments made in crypto are non-refundable.
    
5.  To request a refund, [contact customer supportenvelope](https://doc.anytype.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#17747665725776796e636e6772397e78)
     with your transaction details and reason for the refund.
    

[PreviousMembershipschevron-left](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/monetization)
[NextFeatureschevron-right](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/feature-list-by-platform)

# Sidebar | Anytype Docs

Your sidebar is divided into three sections:

Your channel widget, which includes the Search button, Members button, and Settings button.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-3a0bf0b0e59a8e0f87915bd2f5522e3902535305%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9131b584&sv=2)

The Pinned section where you can find any object that you wish to pin to your sidebar.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-5281330c1f51c988fac74938fb750d8b6196d176%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=96d96a8c&sv=2)

The Objects section which allows you to view all your types, and by extension, all your objects.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-81067a24180ce2c82572c1676c9cc5d9ad824048%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2894b208&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/customize-and-edit-the-sidebar#pinning-objects)

Pinning Objects

In general, you can pin any object that you've created using the Anytype editor to the sidebar. To do so, navigate to the pin button in the top right corner.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-393febb2f498ef458d39497eed00cfce6047cb17%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1d9e18a3&sv=2)

You can unlink them by clicking the same button or right-clicking on them in the pinned section and selecting this option:

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-f2ef65c32f76bde515bd84fd88d597606dbafed2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ff53171&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/customize-and-edit-the-sidebar#adjust-your-widget-appearance)

Adjust your Widget Appearance

Depending on the object type, you can choose from a variety of layouts.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-1dffb2a11af6b73e43519c4241e8a314a42d041d%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=38a82271&sv=2)

Regular objects can choose between compact and tree layouts, while queries and collections can choose from compact, list, compact list, or object layouts.

Selecting the object layout allows you to choose any view from that particular query/collection, and it will also follow that view's layout.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-bca770421ae726da524b977fa15e5120203bea5b%252Fe470b74a31cba9b89fb8f3f4adeadb22149b3a92.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=882fdccf&sv=2)

[PreviousCollectionschevron-left](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/sets/collections)
[NextCollaborationchevron-right](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/collaboration)

Last updated 3 months ago

*   [Pinning Objects](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/customize-and-edit-the-sidebar#pinning-objects)

# Chats | Anytype Docs

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/chats#chat-as-a-channel)

Chat as a Channel

Chat is a new type of channel in Anytype, designed for fast, conversational flow.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-55b3234e1de0c8ccffab6ec1f8ab4803d908db37%252Fchat.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ece9723&sv=2)

It gives you the familiar rhythm of chatting – replying, reacting, sharing files – but with a powerful twist: you can create and edit objects together in real time.

*   Create Objects right from your chat window – turn thoughts into Pages, Tasks, or any other Type.
    
*   Share existing Objects – anything you drop into Chat can be opened and edited right away.
    
*   Keep things organized – uploads are added to the relevant Types (Audio, Images) and everything stays searchable and structured in your sidebar.
    
*   Invite with ease – bring new members into a conversation instantly with links that don’t require approval.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/chats#multi-chats-in-your-space)

Multi-Chats in your Space

Space Channels now hold more than one conversation at a time. Start topic-specific chats right where your work happens – discussions now live alongside your notes, tasks, and documentation as part of your knowledge graph.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fanytype-static.fra1.cdn.digitaloceanspaces.com%2Fimg%2Fhelp%2F51%2F1.png%3Fv%3D0.51.12-alpha&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4fa9b06a&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/chats#chat-as-an-object-type)

Chat as an Object Type

Chats are now native Objects in your Space. You can organize them into different views, assign tags to group related conversations, include them in Collections or Queries, and @-mention them from any Object for cross-referencing. As a system Type, Chat doesn’t support templates or layout changes.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fanytype-static.fra1.cdn.digitaloceanspaces.com%2Fimg%2Fhelp%2F51%2F2.png%3Fv%3D0.51.12-alpha&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=506baf6b&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/chats#widget-behaviour)

Widget Behaviour

The Chats Type Widget works like any other widget: you can pin it to your Sidebar, adjust its appearance by choosing how many chats to show, and pin individual chats for quicker access.Unlike other Widgets, pinned chats display counters and mention indicators directly in the Sidebar. A temporary _Unread_ section also appears automatically when new messages arrive, listing chats with unread content.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fanytype-static.fra1.cdn.digitaloceanspaces.com%2Fimg%2Fhelp%2F51%2F3.png%3Fv%3D0.51.12-alpha&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c84ad654&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/chats#per-chat-notifications)

Per-Chat Notifications

Right-click any Chat Object, or use the three-dots menu inside a chat window to open preferences and choose _Enable all_, _Mentions only_, or _Disable all_.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fanytype-static.fra1.cdn.digitaloceanspaces.com%2Fimg%2Fhelp%2F51%2F4.png%3Fv%3D0.51.12-alpha&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9d2ef22d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/chats#direct-channels)

Direct Channels

Sometimes you just need to talk to one person. Privately.

Direct Channel is a one-on-one connection between two members, where both participants have equal access: no admin, no hierarchy. Just a place for quick check-ins, sharing an object, or whispering memes in the middle of a project. It’s simple, it’s lightweight, and it just works.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fanytype-static.fra1.cdn.digitaloceanspaces.com%2Fimg%2Fhelp%2F52%2F2.png%3Fv%3D0.51.39-alpha&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=34eb69bd&sv=2)

To start a new direct channel, simply click on someone's profile and select 'Send message':

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252FAEFa7kBosXNTlc0O9LDu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D638b4a0d-e71c-43ab-bb63-4ee2240402e6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5b31d69b&sv=2)

[PreviousPublishchevron-left](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/web-publishing)

# Objects | Anytype Docs

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor#what-is-an-object)

What is an Object?

Forget what you already know about knowledge management tools.

At Anytype we have created the concept that everything you create is an Object. Pages, Notes, Recipes, Books, Movies, Audio, Humans, _everything!_

These are all **Objects** that are organized and categorized by **Types**.

You can connect different **Types** by **Properties** and see how this is visualized on the **Graph**.

You will see in your **Settings** that you can create new Types.

In short, an Object is a generalizing term for what you are creating. If it is a page, note, or other Type that you have created.

The Object will be organized by the Type of object that it is.

It is any node in your graph. The smallest linkable unit. Still classified with types.

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor#ways-to-create-objects)

Ways to Create Objects

When clicking the plus button, you’ll immediately create a new object with the type that is set as your default object type in your channel settings.

When clicking the arrow button, you'll be presented with a menu of your types which you can sort to your liking. You can then choose which one you want to create.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252FYxfQXmKEf0X3Hlx9aR5q%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D32284f4a-0b57-4127-ac1e-91d16010e8e7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eca77cdd&sv=2)

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252FwWP9XWNsbLZAk1jyb3jF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc981d9c-049d-44b5-94dd-27b70ac03265&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=783ec80a&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor#command-menu)

Command Menu

When working in the editor you can type `/` to bring up the command menu. If you already know which Type you want to use, you can just type it directly. If you're not sure which Type you want to use, you can type `Objects` instead for the below menu to appear with all of your Types listed. Simply select the Object Type you'd like to create and it will be linked at your current place.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-4cc175ccc7022e337981b2381ed3fefcba2e368e%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e38b4ee0&sv=2)

Command menu > Objects

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor#use-a-shortcut)

Use a Shortcut

For a quick creation of a new Object, you can use this shortcut: `Cmd / Ctrl + N`

This will perform the same action as clicking the "+" sign in the sidebar.

Additionally, you can use `Cmd / Ctrl + Opt / Alt + N` to perform the same action as clicking the arrow sign in the sidebar.

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor#turn-into-object)

Turn Into Object

If you are working on something in an existing Object and would like to transform only a certain block into an Object, you can do that through the action menu by either:

1.  Hovering to the left side of the block that you are working on and clicking the 3 dots.
    
2.  Using the `Cmd / Ctrl + /` keyboard shortcut.
    

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-aa4da582c15ad7be9ff5f1663f17776084777adc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5701a7e2&sv=2)

Action menu

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor#locating-your-objects)

Locating Your Objects

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor#sidebar-1)

Sidebar

You can now find all your objects in the sidebar, grouped by type.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252FXtW8jDCLRW3vgqmTe4P7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd81a7042-b610-48ba-ba10-7877c16c57f5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a9c824db&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor#graph)

Graph

To find all of your objects and how they are connected, you can look to the [Graph](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/feature-list-by-platform/graph)
 for your main source of truth.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-6f794c80678ac250586c8249ff3452f8416a329f%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2ad88d93&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor#search)

Search

To navigate to the search, either head to your sidebar, and click on the search button or use the `Cmd / Ctrl + K` keyboard shortcut.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-e25f3ec4d79e3c2c0c3ec39aac609c789819dac2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1b0f1deb&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor#bin)

Bin

If you've previously removed some objects from your [Channels](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/vault-and-key/space)
, they will appear in your [Bin](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/data-and-security/data-storage-and-deletion/finding-your-objects)
 unless you've already permanently deleted them.

# Queries | Anytype Docs

Lots of people compare Queries with databases, but there's a key difference: Queries don't _store_ Objects like regular databases.

Queries are a way to see a portion of your Graph, and Objects you've created, based on your filtered criteria, and several secondary filters which you can customize. You can think of them as a live filter or query for Objects which share certain criteria - specifically, a Type or a Property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/sets#queries-serve-two-primary-functions)

Queries serve two primary functions:

1.  **Organizing and Accessing Objects** We often get requests along the lines of: _How do I find all of the Notes I've created?_ One easy way is to create a Query based on Type. For example; Note, which will display every Note you've created in Anytype. If you have specific notes you'd like to frequently access, you can filter them based on Properties you've added to these notes. For instance: Creation Date, Tags, or Priority. You can then create a Widget which will appear in your Sidebar, acting like a folder for all Objects that meet certain criteria.
    
2.  **Editing Objects**
    

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-569af642084351c2daed228a43386deae497bc0a%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b9c4adfc&sv=2)

Queries also provide a way to quickly edit Objects in a list View. You can use multi-select in Queries to delete multiple Objects at once, or to batch update Properties / the Object Type of Objects. Any Properties added to a Query in the Property Menu (top right), will be adopted by all new Objects created with the "+ New Object" button.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-9e35d1be3a5c337762217dde03ddbdfa4c993c7e%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8fd95091&sv=2)

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-b0a632bed3210118e16ed798aa149581ea0daec1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4e4b81d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/sets#creating-queries)

Creating Queries

You can create a new Query with the drop-down button from your sidebar or using the / shortcut menu in the editor.

You'll then need to choose if you want a Query by Type which lets you list all of your Objects of a certain Type, or a Query by Property which will list all Objects that contain the Property of your choosing.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-b11e6f9fc00a4c7627f2c73ac983383f351640f7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a8f12b41&sv=2)

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-0fd84da26d26f81f5a7d8abc0c1d10ec2369b87b%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ecff7b80&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/sets#customizing-your-query)

Customizing Your Query

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/sets#toggle-and-add-properties-to-objects-via-queries)

Toggle & Add Properties to Objects via Queries

Instead of adding Properties one-by-one to Objects, you can batch-add them to your Query by clicking the filters on the right side.

Here you can toggle on/off any Properties that you would like to see, add another Property or new Property, and edit the View of the Query here.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-b8cfd13af407131570d2392f78879bb80fb13829%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7eef4ea5&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/sets#sorts-and-filters)

Sorts & Filters

You are also able to sort or filter your Query by any Property that you've previously added to the Query.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-37065722031925e83e716c3d7b49de56f6b6904c%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b3e233a&sv=2)

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-7327eb3120412e1dd31ec651b0e868afed4b51aa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2390945d&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/sets#layout)

Layout

In this section you can find all the currently available layout options.

circle-exclamation

Kanban, calendar and graph views are available on desktop only.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-8caf4f05638ae6432e8ce4e6f5571016cb789f8e%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bb3675d9&sv=2)

# Templates | Anytype Docs

Templates are one of our most-beloved ways to work at Anytype, designed to help you scale and personalize your Object creation flows. With Templates, you can:

*   Customize the cover or icon you want to use to for certain object Types
    
*   Automatically re-use the same structure each time you add a new Object
    

Templates are saved on the Type level, and each Type can support multiple Templates. For example, you can have different Templates for different kinds of Books, like academic, fiction, or non-fiction.

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/types/templates#how-to-create-a-template)

How to Create a Template

There are three ways to add a Template:

1) Navigate to `Channel > Content Model > Object Types` → Click the Type for which you'd like to create a Template → Click on Templates in the top right corner → Click + to start creating a new template → Give your Template a name and start adding Properties and formatting → Your Template is auto-saved

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-c3ff1d780cb35621cd4f969f76bc195869ab1945%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=50b34694&sv=2)

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-254cafa022463dbf179168d0ff484ed055443c5d%252Fimage%2520%28165%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7f91dd74&sv=2)

You can also manage templates directly from the Edit Type menu, accessible from every object.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-35920b0a70da8282c5c25c88af7910f5766b3406%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e2df7213&sv=2)

2) If you're working within an Object and would like to save your work as a Template, you can: Navigate to `···` in the top-right corner → Click + Use as a Template, and your content will automatically be saved as a new Template for this Object Type.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-b0348363757979d053a9179f2bb12b0814940b17%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=655b6896&sv=2)

3) If you are working in a List and you would like to create / edit your templates, you can: Navigate to `New|▾` in the top-right corner of the List view -> Click on the `▾` button to open up the template modal. Then either create a new template by using the `+` button, or modify an existing one by clicking on `···` in the top right corner of the template button, and choosing either `Edit template`, `Duplicate` or `Delete`.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-09878aa8f353d2097e44bb99f86fa16f62ad8cae%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f70b531&sv=2)

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-331d4bdadc1a56c2ea46902ed6fc4c98c5e70f24%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=850b7f1d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/types/templates#using-and-managing-templates)

Using & Managing Templates

Depending on the way you've created your new object, either the default template will be applied automatically, or you will be asked to choose a template yourself.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-5ead26fb505f72b28e085ed797c57d17c014306e%252F5_Template%2520Picker%2520Screenshot.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=99fadf65&sv=2)

Choose a template

You can also choose the default template for each type by opening the Type object, or you can choose the default template for each List view.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-4f106fda7b00a34839fdcf1cf31296bfede709bd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7938c6a2&sv=2)

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-752b86b05dc81f632fcc32df11dc5959159884a3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b40cc244&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/types/templates#template-name-pre-fill)

Template Name Pre-fill

When editing a template, a new toggle lets you choose whether the template's name is pre-filled when creating Objects from it, so you no longer need to manually clear inherited names.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Ft6cOxduYwJPexJ6CZOz3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df0efb4de-8afc-4d84-b2cd-9e7abf05000a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=77835186&sv=2)

[PreviousPropertieschevron-left](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/types/relations)
[NextQuerieschevron-right](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/sets)

Last updated 1 month ago

Was this helpful?

# Dates | Anytype Docs

You can open any date as a separate object and view the entire context related to that date.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-cce6c5227da6c86ac0e0604e6afb8d22f9679f39%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2f9a1767&sv=2)

This includes [mentions (@date)](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor/linking-objects#date-mentions)
, automatically created dates and custom date properties.

Date is also accessible from properties, layouts, graph, calendar view and more.

[PreviousCustom CSSchevron-left](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/feature-list-by-platform/custom-css)
[NextGraphchevron-right](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/feature-list-by-platform/graph)

# Graph | Anytype Docs

circle-exclamation

Available on desktop only.

From anywhere in the app, you'll see the graph icon at the top and next to your sidebar:

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-2635f053c305e4739945cedbce6a59d5e11b85c8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f048549&sv=2)

In the Graph you can see which Objects are connected together, and the direction everything flows.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-977562c545ef064b626ce5d64b8bfea706cd121a%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=233253b1&sv=2)

On the top right of the screen in your Graph, you can **search** and optimize some settings.

Toggle appearances for title, arrows, and icons.

Optimize viewing links, Properties, and unlinked objects. **If you are missing some objects, check to show unlinked objects.**

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-f41c3bdbaa77d7ff9cf6b3ea260b50280469d2c7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2a96e7e&sv=2)

[PreviousDateschevron-left](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/feature-list-by-platform/dates)
[NextOther Featureschevron-right](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/feature-list-by-platform/other-features)

# Raycast Extension (macOS) | Anytype Docs

Our long-awaited API is beginning to take shape! The first step is Raycast integration, allowing you to create, read, and delete Channels, Objects, and Types, as well as search across them, all from Raycast on macOS.

[Install the Raycast Extension herearrow-up-right](https://www.raycast.com/any/anytype)

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-9a1730d828ff1b13e000df8e72efb0f604ff53b7%252Fraycast_2x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8a5ea509&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/feature-list-by-platform/local-api/raycast-extension-macos#update-ai)

Update - AI

We've introduced several enhancements based on your requests and feedback, plus Anytype for Raycast is now an AI Extension – search through channels and objects using natural language or create new ones just by instructing @anytype.

*   Improved Pinning & Navigation: Pin objects, types, members and channels for quicker access. Objects of a certain Type now appear below their templates for better organization.
    
*   Better Collection Management: Create objects directly within collections and browse collection items with ease.
    
*   Customization & Visibility: Choose Open Object in Anytype as the default action, show custom properties in the Detail sidebar, toggle metadata in object details and apply templates when creating new objects.
    

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-7b617d7b283ea52be7eba0068b87ed6abac8291c%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-17%2520at%252011.43.00%25E2%2580%25AFAM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1a2e7776&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/feature-list-by-platform/local-api/raycast-extension-macos#update-local-api)

Update - Local API

As a companion to our Local API, we’ve just shipped great improvements for our Raycast extension.

Here’s what’s new:

*   **Quickly create** new channels, objects, types, properties, or tags with the shortcut `CMD+N` while browsing your channels.
    
*   **Easily edit** your selected items (channels, objects, types, properties or tags) using `CMD+E`.
    
*   **Conveniently add objects** to lists either through the new `Add object to list` command or directly from the context menu `CMD+K`.
    

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-d42eab6407742667eb9d2bc24ae61373f7f9854e%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cd56a129&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/feature-list-by-platform/local-api/raycast-extension-macos#privacy)

Privacy

Our API runs locally on your machine, works without internet connection and requires authentication for a client (eg. raycast extension) to retrieve & access data.

To accomplish this, Raycast initially pairs with the app through the 4 digit pop-up. This notifies you about giving the extension limited access to your account.

The API key is stored in encrypted local storage of the extension and will be used to fetch data from the app (to display channels, objects etc.).

Therefore, no other applications than the authorized ones can access your data through the API.

[PreviousLocal APIchevron-left](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/feature-list-by-platform/local-api)
[NextCustom CSSchevron-right](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/feature-list-by-platform/custom-css)

Last updated 3 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Update - AI](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/feature-list-by-platform/local-api/raycast-extension-macos#update-ai)
    
*   [Update - Local API](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/feature-list-by-platform/local-api/raycast-extension-macos#update-local-api)
    
*   [Privacy](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/feature-list-by-platform/local-api/raycast-extension-macos#privacy)

# Links | Anytype Docs

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor/linking-objects#creating-new-links)

Creating New Links

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor/linking-objects#link-to-another-object-in-anytype)

Link to another Object in Anytype

Directly through the editor by using:

1.  **Block Links.** Type "/" to invoke a command bar, and then look for the `Link to Object` option in the menu. These can appear either as text or as cards.
    
2.  **Inline Links**. Type @ or \[\[ to invoke the Object picker menu.\
    \
\
![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-1264bc3d7dd1c75091ca5c0971e36b00d532da13%252Fimage%2520%2816%29%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a32980f1&sv=2)\
\
Link Blocks\
\
![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-2275c770ead814d7dd49a5591a35fdfa0fbee4b0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d8b53ec2&sv=2)\
\
Inline Mentions\
\
With Properties by assigning an Object Property Type in the Object menu.\
\
![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-75803b84ee5f5ce95863a9414795e81cf051d6d0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b5ec51aa&sv=2)\
\
#### \
\
[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor/linking-objects#link-to-external-object-on-your-device)\
\
Link to external Object on your device\
\
If you want to add a link to an external Object on your desktop, please use the links starting with **file:///** plus the local file destination. For example:\
\
*   `file:///Users/Filip/Downloads/Protocol-Berg.pdf` — to open PDFs;\
    \
*   `file:///Users/Filip/Downloads/my_budget.xlsx` — to open spreadsheets (Excel, Numbers).\
    \
\
To add such a link, pick up "Link to website" just like when you add a new link to a website.\
\
#### \
\
[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor/linking-objects#date-mentions)\
\
Date mentions\
\
You can use **Inline Links** to quickly link to either absolute or relative dates.\
\
Some examples:\
\
*   @now or @today\
    \
*   @tomorrow\
    \
*   @nextweek\
    \
*   @nextmonth\
    \
*   @24/8/2023\
    \
\
It's also possible to use `@date` or `/date` to quickly open the date selection menu.\
\
![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-45cc9e847b5683aa3dadf3811b89e05c3cc33985%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9d18c071&sv=2)\
\
#### \
\
[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor/linking-objects#link-aliases)\
\
Link aliases\
\
You can use regular links to link to a specific object in your space using a different name.\
\
1.  Write the name of your link first.\
    \
2.  Select the name and press `Cmd / Ctrl + Shift + K`.\
    \
3.  Search for the object you want to link, and select it.\
    \
\
### \
\
[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor/linking-objects#checking-existing-links)\
\
Checking Existing Links\
\
#### \
\
[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor/linking-objects#properties-on-the-graph)\
\
Properties on the Graph\
\
In your documents you may have multiple references or connections which could be attached to other work in your library. The Graph is the visualizer for this. Objects connected to other Objects, connected to Humans, or Tasks.\
\
Learn more about [Properties](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/types/relations)\
 & the [Graph](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/feature-list-by-platform/graph)\
 here.\
\
#### \
\
[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor/linking-objects#use-the-flow)\
\
Use the Flow\
\
![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-15c9c8ad22ba60268c2a5e96a785d8a46cf8fa06%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9602c3b5&sv=2)\
\
Another option to check which Objects are linked together can be found in the Flow tab next to the Graph.\
\
On the top, center of your screen you will see the option to toggle to **Flow** view. This will show you which Object is linked before and after the current Object you are viewing.\
\
#### \
\
[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/object-editor/linking-objects#backlinks)\
\
Backlinks\
\
![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-89910015cbd60ddcd3820c43af4aa9c6177f5211%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=381babae&sv=2)\
\
Lastly, you can use the Backlinks property to check which Objects link to the currently opened one.\
\

[NextTypeschevron-right](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/types)\

# Install | Anytype Docs

You can download the latest version of Anytype for your device at [download.anytype.ioarrow-up-right](https://download.anytype.io/)
.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-42b6c6c3fab58bcd3408849834daccda62a238b5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f93c8045&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/install-and-setup#create-your-vault)

Create your vault

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-b684a931e58a67106354e403b615ae779580e03f%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bb5cb0d0&sv=2)

If you haven't created a vault yet, you can easily create one by clicking on `I am new here` and then following the provided instructions.

**Language:** If you would like to use a language other than English for the interface, you can select it in the top right corner.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-c8c2193d7147ad3f45b99d70c7d38bd177054034%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7f4194bd&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/install-and-setup#save-your-key)

Save your Key!

triangle-exclamation

Make sure you store your [Key](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/vault-and-key/key)
 somewhere safe, and try not to share it with anyone who can't be trusted!

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-31745ce02978a3838de425a5c4bfb800c3338e76%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b26e835b&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/install-and-setup#stay-in-the-loop)

Stay in the loop

Enter your email address to receive tips and tricks from the Anytype team.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-ec7878e675aae997d71ca4fb42d5019f8d1c4559%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d003f264&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/install-and-setup#share-a-bit-about-yourself)

Share a bit about yourself

Help us build and improve Anytype by telling us how you plan to use it.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-f507d090193b4a7a4e8f757e7a610392b2d1cef6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e999b69b&sv=2)

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-f8226e77192a4ee08c12b7a7ace2c72089548f96%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4e0ddf9a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/install-and-setup#log-in-using-your-key)

Log-in using your Key

On the contrary, if you already have a vault, click on `I already have a Key` and enter your [Key](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/vault-and-key/key)
 to proceed.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-bb96d3c5aff0100b4be2044109c78c6a985f955e%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=74a88c9a&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/install-and-setup#log-in-using-the-qr-code)

Log-in using the QR code

In addition to using your [Key](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/vault-and-key/key)
 to log in, you can also use the QR code to login faster if your desktop is close by.

To log in using the QR code, simply navigate to [Login Key](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/settings/account-and-data#login-key)
 in your Vault Settings.

![](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2112047522-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJbcKxgThRdSa4vZyLbvH%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-66e635c65e3d3a6759166e531b1ccc5955c79a55%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9055f11c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/getting-started/install-and-setup#import)

Import

If you would like to import some of your existing data into your Space, you can find the instructions on how to do so in [Import](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/data-and-security/import-export#import)
.

# Migrate from Obsidian | Anytype Docs

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/data-and-security/import-export/migrate-from-obsidian#step-1-export-from-obsidian)

Step 1: Export from Obsidian

*   Clean up your notes
    
    *   Convert embeds like `![[Note Title]]` into simple links `[[Note Title]]`
        
    *   Remove or convert plugin-specific syntax, such as Dataview queries, Templater fields, etc.
        
    
*   Locate your vault
    
    *   Open the Vault switcher (shown at launch or via `File → Open Vault`).
        
    *   Right-click the vault you want to export and choose “Reveal in system explorer.”
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/data-and-security/import-export/migrate-from-obsidian#step-2-import-into-anytype)

Step 2: Import into Anytype

*   Open `Channel Settings → Import → Obsidian` and click on Import files.
    
*   Select your vault folder (or a subfolder) for import.
    
    *   On some platforms (like Linux and Windows), folder selection may not be supported. In that case, compress the folder into a .zip archive and import the archive instead.
        
    
*   Anytype will process the contents and automatically create a separate object for each Markdown file.
    

circle-info

**Content mapping**

*   `[[Internal Links]]` → become linked objects in Anytype, so the connections between your notes are preserved.
    
*   `#tags` → become values in the Tag property. You can use them to filter, group or search across objects.
    
*   Frontmatter (the `---` metadata at the top) → becomes object properties.
    

[PreviousImport & Exportchevron-left](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/data-and-security/import-export)
[NextMigrate from Notionchevron-right](https://doc.anytype.io/anytype-docs/advanced/data-and-security/import-export/migrate-from-notion)
